about_this_resource_text: "<p><strong>Description:</strong> Among all graphs with\
  \ a given edge density, which graph has the maximum/minimum triangle density? Professor\
  \ Zhao explains extremal problems on subgraph densities using the framework of graph\
  \ limits.\r\n\r\n</p>\r\n<p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Yufei Zhao</p>"

  <span m="682860">if</span> <span m="683010">you</span> <span m="683100">know</span>
  <span m="683360">this</span> <span m="683550">inequality</span> <span m="684910">and</span>
  <span m="685410">everything</span> <span m="685700">is</span> <span m="685800">continuous,</span>
  <span m="687100">then</span> <span m="687450">you</span> <span m="687600">know</span>
  <span m="687780">that</span> <span m="687960">inequality.</span> <span m="689290">So</span>

  <span m="690600">other.</span></p><p><span m="692240">Now,</span> <span m="692490">with</span>

  <span m="1011610">to</span> <span m="1011700">the</span> <span m="1011790">spectrum.</span>

  <span m="4363670">And</span> <span m="4363760">now</span> <span m="4364330">I</span>
  <span m="4364450">start</span> <span m="4364900">with--</span> <span m="4366600">I</span>
  <span m="4366690">can</span> <span m="4366990">reduce</span> <span m="4367500">the</span>
  <span m="4367590">problem</span> <span m="4368430">to</span> <span m="4368820">the</span>
  <span m="4368970">problem</span> <span m="4369330">of</span> <span m="4370230">decidability</span>
  <span m="4371070">of</span> <span m="4371970">integer</span> <span m="4372840">inequalities.</span></p><p><span
  m="4374510">I</span> <span m="4374760">start</span> <span m="4375080">with</span>
  <span m="4375270">an</span> <span m="4375450">integer</span> <span m="4375810">inequality.</span>
  <span m="4377220">I</span> <span m="4377670">convert</span> <span m="4378135">it</span>
  <span m="4379170">to</span> <span m="4379420">an</span> <span m="4379560">inequality</span>
  <span m="4380880">about</span> <span m="4381480">points</span> <span m="4382360">on</span>
  <span m="4382620">this</span> <span m="4382830">red</span> <span m="4383070">curve.</span>
  <span m="4385990">And</span> <span m="4388380">that</span> <span m="4388610">turns</span>
  <span m="4389030">into</span> <span m="4390140">a</span> <span m="4390200">corresponding</span>
  <span m="4391190">graph</span> <span m="4391940">inequality,</span> <span m="4394170">which</span>
  <span m="4394440">must</span> <span m="4394710">then</span> <span m="4394950">be</span>
  <span m="4395160">undecidable.</span> <span m="4399020">So</span> <span m="4399250">this</span>
  <span m="4399470">undecidability</span> <span m="4400120">result</span> <span m="4400480">is</span>
  <span m="4400660">related</span> <span m="4401080">to</span> <span m="4401290">the</span>
  <span m="4401360">discreteness</span> <span m="4402970">of</span> <span m="4403390">points</span>
  <span m="4403780">on</span> <span m="4404560">this</span> <span m="4404740">red</span>
  <span m="4404950">curve.</span></p><p><span m="4409990">So</span> <span m="4410240">general</span>
  <span m="4410600">undecidability</span> <span m="4411350">results</span> <span m="4411640">are</span>
  <span m="4411740">interesting.</span> <span m="4412370">But</span> <span m="4412730">often,</span>
  <span m="4412950">we're</span> <span m="4413120">interested</span> <span m="4413540">in</span>

  <span m="4415340">I</span> <span m="4415400">give</span> <span m="4415580">you</span>

  <span m="4417800">it</span> <span m="4417860">true?</span> <span m="4418970">And</span>

  <span m="4421520">open</span> <span m="4421790">problems</span> <span m="4422720">of</span>

  <span m="4727510">check</span> <span m="4728200">over</span> <span m="4728560">all</span>
  <span m="4729710">weighted</span> <span m="4730180">graphs</span> <span m="4731270">on</span>
  <span m="4731620">some</span> <span m="4731860">bounded</span> <span m="4732160">number</span>
  <span m="4732370">of</span> <span m="4732700">parts</span> <span m="4733030">whose</span>
  <span m="4734260">edge weights</span> <span m="4734740">are</span> <span m="4734860">multiples</span>
  <span m="4735460">of</span> <span m="4735610">epsilon,</span> <span m="4736120">let's</span>
  <span m="4736300">say,</span> <span m="4737530">whether</span> <span m="4737800">this</span>
  <span m="4737980">is</span> <span m="4738100">true.</span> <span m="4739330">If</span>
  <span m="4739420">it's</span> <span m="4739570">true,</span> <span m="4739780">then</span>
  <span m="4739960">it</span> <span m="4740010">is</span> <span m="4740110">true</span>
  <span m="4740290">with</span> <span m="4741050">this</span> <span m="4741220">epsilon.</span>
  <span m="4742090">If</span> <span m="4742210">it</span> <span m="4742300">is</span>
  <span m="4742450">false,</span> <span m="4742910">then</span> <span m="4743050">I</span>
  <span m="4743110">can</span> <span m="4743290">already</span> <span m="4743560">output</span>
  <span m="4744130">a</span> <span m="4744190">counterexample.</span></p><p><span
  m="4746860">So</span> <span m="4746980">there</span> <span m="4747100">is</span>
  <span m="4747220">only</span> <span m="4747400">finitely</span> <span m="4747820">many</span>
  <span m="4748030">possibilities</span> <span m="4748870">as</span> <span m="4749020">a</span>
  <span m="4749050">result</span> <span m="4749420">of</span> <span m="4749520">weak</span>
  <span m="4749620">regularity</span> <span m="4750190">lemma.</span> <span m="4751090">And</span>
  <span m="4751390">therefore,</span> <span m="4752770">this</span> <span m="4752980">version</span>
  <span m="4753280">here</span> <span m="4753520">is</span> <span m="4753670">decidable.</span>
  <span m="4755870">So</span> <span m="4757040">today,</span> <span m="4757310">we</span>
  <span m="4757460">saw</span> <span m="4757730">many</span> <span m="4758000">different</span>
  <span m="4758420">graph</span> <span m="4758790">theoretic</span> <span m="4759200">inequalities</span>
  <span m="4760190">and</span> <span m="4760340">some</span> <span m="4760550">general</span>
  <span m="4760850">results.</span> <span m="4761520">And</span> <span m="4761570">there</span>
  <span m="4761660">are</span> <span m="4761720">lots</span> <span m="4761960">of</span>
  <span m="4762080">open</span> <span m="4762320">problems</span> <span m="4763730">about</span>
  <span m="4764480">graph</span> <span m="4764780">homomorphism</span> <span m="4765470">inequalities.</span></p><p><span
  m="4767210">So</span> <span m="4767510">this</span> <span m="4767750">concludes</span>
  <span m="4768950">roughly</span> <span m="4769370">the</span> <span m="4769860">extremal</span>
  <span m="4770360">graph</span> <span m="4770790">theory</span> <span m="4771055">section</span>
  <span m="4771320">of</span> <span m="4771410">this</span> <span m="4771560">course.</span>
  <span m="4772020">So</span> <span m="4772100">starting</span> <span m="4772460">from</span>
  <span m="4772640">next</span> <span m="4772940">lecture,</span> <span m="4773760">we'll</span>
  <span m="4773810">be</span> <span m="4773930">looking</span> <span m="4774290">at</span>
  <span m="4774950">Roth's</span> <span m="4775400">theorem.</span> <span m="4776130">So</span>
  <span m="4776300">looking</span> <span m="4776630">at</span> <span m="4776760">the</span>
